\doxysubsubsection*{tick\+Raw \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}br\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}
Process the encoder tick without clearing the turn flag.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em state} & the current state of the encoder \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1, 0, or 1 based on the direction of rotation 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A class that represents an encoder button. 

This class extends the \doxylink{class_virt_enc_button}{Virt\+Enc\+Button} class and provides additional functionality for handling an encoder button. It allows initializing the encoder pins, button pin, and button mode. It also provides methods for reading the button state and encoder value. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{core_2_enc_button_8h_source_l00020}{20}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{core_2_enc_button_8h_source}{Enc\+Button.\+h}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pressFor()}{pressFor()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_virt_button_a5dc04d5d164a4fea978b9004daf23de0}{uint16\+\_\+t}} Virt\+Button\+::press\+For (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the duration in milliseconds for which the button has been pressed. If the EB\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+PEDOMETER macro is defined, the function always returns 0. If the button is not currently pressed, the function also returns 0.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The duration in milliseconds for which the button has been pressed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
